<rate>5<//rate>< review>
My experience with Andrew Lewis Homes went as expected. They got the job done in a timely and professional manner.

Garrett Schwarz was my realtor: he was young and ready to hit the ground running. He did well under pressure, and listened to my grievances as they came up. Garrett was very familiar with Riverside and San Diego county communities.

<review>I was recommended to take my used tires here to get them mounted by Fred over at Atlantis Tire. The workers are nice decent people who seem to care and have good prices. However, their equipment for mounting and dismounting tires is no good for aluminum and painted wheels. I had a total of 6 tires dismounted and all my aluminum wheels have 4 of these marks on the inside surface.

Furthermore, when the technician used the pry bar to get the tire off or on he also scuffed up the visible surface of my wheels. The woman in the office who seems to be the manager was off to lunch when this happened so all they could offer my was an apology.

Finally, when the wheels were placed back on the technician used an pneumatic impact wrench to torque the lug nuts down. That is a big no-no as they should be properly torqued down using a torque wrench. I had to ask him to properly retorque the wheels. The tech came out with a colored torque socket. These are known to be less reliable than a calibrated torque wrench. Moreover, those sockets can lead to overtightening and damaged wheel studs. As soon as I got home I retorqued my lugs properly with a torque wrench.

I have been to many tire shops and this is the first time my wheels have been damaged by one. To the owner - please invest in proper equipment so that you do not damage people's wheels and please take the time to properly torque down lug nuts by hand.<//review><Pics>[{'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipMicz9OrG7SjEDKQCkMiSBMOi05mYdPPvdn8WJz=w150-h150-k-no-p']}, {'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipNzdFcgJ_L2Xt2LM-CMhJAt9ZJ6U7yFtiEGGwRy=w150-h150-k-no-p']}, {'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipNfybNyUjX9ljOhsNj1XR4YquqSAIt6cSKchQdj=w150-h150-k-no-p']}, {'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipPcN_GP3tu-rhaCbJQ5Purein5s9buCtsxoBxsm=w150-h150-k-no-p']}, {'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipMd2vtHV4iej9uy-aHTshCqKfmKOgmFN62gsbdo=w150-h150-k-no-p']}, {'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipNlZOb8kgzWQyXM_tNuUzd_cJEStTGQn0Mp4QHt=w150-h150-k-no-p']}]<//Pics><Response>None<//Response>< gmapID>
